**GT: -0.0834*v³ - 0.9954*log(|v| + 1) + 0.7824*sin(t)**

The GT has three basis functions:
1. **v³** (cubic in v)
2. **log(|v| + 1)** (logarithmic in |v|)
3. **sin(t)** (sinusoidal in t)

Let me analyze each candidate to see if it can match these three terms exactly.

**Key observations:**
- The GT has no exponential terms in t (no exp(c*t))
- The GT has no polynomial terms in t
- The GT has log(|v| + 1), which is a specific nonlinear function of v
- The GT has v³ and sin(t)

For candidates with exp(c1*t) terms, I can set c1=0 to make them constants. Similarly, terms like c0*t can be zeroed by setting c0=0.

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*v + c3*v³ + c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*v*sin(c8*t+c9)
Setting c1=0 (constant), c7=0 (kill v*sin term), c2=0: gives constant + c3*v³ + c4*sin(c5*t+c6). Missing log(|v|+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** Similar - has v, v³, sin, exp, cos(exp). No log term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** Has v³, exp(sin), v terms. No log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** v*cos(t), sin, v, v³. No log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** c0 + c1*v³ + c2*v + c3*v*log(c4*|v|+1) + c5*sin(c6*t+c7) + c8*v³*exp(c9*|v|)
This has v*log(c4*|v|+1), not log(|v|+1). These are different functions. v*log(|v|+1) ≠ log(|v|+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** c1*v³ + c2*v³ + c3*v + c4*v*log(c5*|v|+1) + c6*sin(c7*t+c8) + c9*v
Has v*log(c5*|v|+1), not log(|v|+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 7-20:** Let me check each for log(|v|+1) or equivalent...

Most candidates have combinations of v, v³, v*|v|, sin(t), exp(t), etc. None have log(|v|+1).

**Candidate 21:** c1*v*log(c2*|v|+1) + ... Has v*log, not log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 33:** Same issue - v*log, not log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 36:** c3*sin(c4*log(c5*|v|+1) + c6) - has sin(log(|v|+1)), not log(|v|+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** c2*v + c3*v³ + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t+c7)) + c8*|v| + c0*t/(c1+t²)
Has v, v³, |v|, exp(sin(t)), t/(1+t²). No log. **NO MATCH**

Going through ALL 50 candidates systematically, none contain a bare **log(|v| + c)** term. They have:
- v*log(|v|+1) (Candidates 5, 6, 21, 33)
- sin(log(|v|+1)) (Candidate 36)
- Various combinations of v, v³, v*|v|, sin, cos, exp

Since log(|v|+1) is linearly independent from v, v³, v*|v|, v*log(|v|+1), and all other basis functions present in the candidates, none of these candidates can exactly reproduce the GT.
